<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Results of Operation and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">On February&#160;7, 2022, ON Semiconductor Corporation announced in a news release its financial performance for the fourth quarter and year ended December&#160;31, 2021 and other related material information (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Earnings Release</span></span>&#8221;). A copy of the Earnings Release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">The information in Item&#160;2.02 of this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> including Exhibit 99.1, is being furnished under Item&#160;2.02 and shall not be deemed to be &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Exchange Act</span></span>&#8221;), or otherwise subject to liability under that section, nor shall such information be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>onsemi Reports Fourth Quarter and 2021 Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:15pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Achieved record annual and quarterly revenue, gross margin, profit and cash flow </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>PHOENIX, Ariz. &#150; Feb. 7, 2022 &#150;</B> <B>onsemi</B> (the &#147;Company&#148;) (Nasdaq: ON) today announced its fourth quarter and fiscal year 2021
results with the following highlights: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="12%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Record fiscal year revenue of $6.74&nbsp;billion representing 28.3&nbsp;% year-over-year growth
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:3pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="12%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Record quarterly revenue of $1,846.1&nbsp;million, and record GAAP and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross margins of 45.1&nbsp;% and 45.2&nbsp;%, respectively </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:3pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="12%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Record quarterly GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating margins of 26.0&nbsp;%
and 28.6&nbsp;%, respectively </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:3pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="12%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Fourth quarter GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share of $0.96
and $1.09, respectively </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="12%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">2021 free cash flow increased 167&nbsp;% year-over-year, with fourth quarter at $457.0&nbsp;million or
25&nbsp;% of revenue </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">&#147;Our disciplined execution on transformation initiatives in 2021 resulted in record financial
performance and achievement of our financial targets ahead of stated timeline. Revenue for 2021 grew 28.3&nbsp;%. Operating income and free cash flow increased 6 times faster than the revenue as we focus our portfolio on secular megatrends of
electric vehicles, ADAS, alternative energy and industrial automation. We continue to expand gross margins as we shift our mix into these high-value strategic markets while ramping new products, rationalizing our manufacturing footprint, and
improving our overall cost structure. Outlook for our business remains robust as evidenced by over 60&nbsp;% year-over-year growth in our design win funnel driven by our highly differentiated intelligent power and sensing portfolio,&#148; said
Hassane <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">El-Khoury,</FONT> president and CEO of <B>onsemi.</B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:30pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>Selected financial results for the
quarter are shown below with comparable periods: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Diluted shares outstanding can vary as a result of, among other things, the vesting of restricted stock
units, the incremental dilutive shares from the Company&#146;s convertible senior subordinated notes, and the repurchase or the issuance of stock or convertible notes or the sale of treasury shares. With the adoption of the new accounting standard,
the GAAP diluted shares outstanding assumes settling the principal and excess over par value in shares of the Company&#146;s common stock for the 1.625% Notes and only the excess over par value in shares of the Company&#146;s common stock for the 0%
Notes, according to the terms of such notes. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted shares outstanding includes the shares that are not covered by the Company&#146;s hedge transaction issued concurrently with such notes. In
periods when the quarterly average stock price exceeds $30.70 for the 1.625% Notes and $74.34 for the 0% Notes, the dilutive impact of the warrants issued concurrently with such notes are included in the GAAP and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted shares outstanding. Calculations are based on the Company&#146;s stock price as of December&nbsp;31, 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

fair market value <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">step-up;</FONT> purchased <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-process</FONT> research and development expenses; restructuring, asset impairments and other, net; goodwill impairment charges; gains
and losses on debt prepayment; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> interest expense; actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits; and certain other special items, as necessary. These special items are out of our
control and could change significantly from period to period. As a result, we are not able to reasonably estimate and separately present the individual impact or probable significance of these special items, and we are similarly unable to provide a
reconciliation of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The reconciliation that is unavailable would include a forward-looking income statement, balance sheet and statement of cash flows in accordance with GAAP.&nbsp;For
this reason, we use a projected range of the aggregate amount of special items in order to calculate our projected <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating expense outlook. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

information to investors. We use these measures, together with GAAP measures, for internal managerial purposes and as a means to evaluate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparisons.
However, we do not, and you should not, rely on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures alone as measures of our performance. We believe that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures reflect an
additional way of viewing aspects of our operations that, when taken together with GAAP results and the reconciliations to corresponding GAAP financial measures that we also provide in our releases, provide a more complete understanding of factors
and trends affecting our business. Because <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these financial measures with other companies&#146;
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, even if they have similar names. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>TELECONFERENCE </B></P>

which is 8631312.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About onsemi </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">onsemi (Nasdaq: ON)
is driving disruptive innovations to help build a better future. With a focus on automotive and industrial <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-markets,</FONT> the company is accelerating change in megatrends such as vehicle electrification and
safety, sustainable energy grids, industrial automation, and 5G and cloud infrastructure. With a highly differentiated and innovative product portfolio, onsemi creates intelligent power and sensing technologies that solve the world&#146;s most
complex challenges and leads the way in creating a safer, cleaner, and smarter world. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"># # # </P>

<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1.30em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(1)</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt">Tax impact of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> special items
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(a-i)</FONT> is calculated using the federal statutory rate of 21% for all periods presented.</P></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="5"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="5" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1.30em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(2)</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt">The Company simplified its corporate structure by repatriating the economic rights of its
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-U.S.</FONT> intellectual property to the United States via domestication of certain foreign subsidiaries (the &#147;Domestication&#148;). The Domestication resulted in a benefit from recognizing certain deferred
tax assets, net of deferred tax liabilities, of $62.9&nbsp;million. Additionally, the Domestication caused the Company to reassess the full valuation allowance recorded against its U.S. state deferred tax assets. As a result, the Company released
approximately $49.5&nbsp;million of its valuation allowance recorded against its U.S. state deferred tax assets.</P></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="5"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="5" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1.30em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(3)</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt">The income tax adjustment primarily represents the use of the net operating loss,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impact of not asserting indefinite reinvestment on earnings of our foreign subsidiaries, deferred tax expense not affecting taxes payable, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expense
(benefit) related to uncertain tax positions.</P></TD></TR>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:20pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">To supplement the consolidated financial results prepared in accordance with GAAP, onsemi uses
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">certain&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> which are adjusted from the most directly comparable GAAP measures to exclude items related to the amortization of intangible assets, amortization of acquisition-related
intangibles, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;inventory</FONT> valuation adjustments, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">purchased&nbsp;in-process</FONT> research and development
expenses, restructuring, asset impairments and other, net, goodwill impairment charges, gains and losses on debt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and
other pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture-related costs, tax impact of these items, and certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">other&nbsp;non-recurring&nbsp;items,</FONT> as necessary. Management does not consider the effects
of these items in evaluating the core operational activities of onsemi. Management uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> internally to make strategic decisions, forecast future results, and evaluate
onsemi&#146;s current performance. In addition, the Company believes that most analysts covering onsemi&#146;s use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP</FONT> measures to evaluate onsemi&#146;s performance. Given management&#146;s and
other relevant use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> onsemi believes these measures are important to investors in understanding onsemi&#146;s current and future operating results as seen through the eyes
of management. In addition, management believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are useful to investors in enabling them to better assess changes in onsemi&#146;s core business across different time periods.
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">These&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are not prepared in accordance with, and should not be considered alternatives or necessarily superior to, GAAP financial data and may be different <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">from&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> used by other companies. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Because&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these financial
measures with other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">companies&#146;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures, even if they have similar names. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Revenue </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> revenue allows management to evaluate, among other things, the revenue from the
Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent of special items. In addition, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> revenue is an important component of management&#146;s
internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future
results. Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of
onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Gross</FONT> Profit and Gross Margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT> profit and gross margin allows management to evaluate, among other
things, the gross margin and gross profit of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally
speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up&nbsp;and</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs. In addition, it is an important component of
management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets, and
forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of revenue
of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Operating</FONT> Income and&nbsp;Operating Margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating</FONT> income and operating margin allows management to evaluate,
among other things, the operating margin and operating income of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT>
including, generally speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;non-recurring</FONT></FONT> facility costs, amortization and impairments of
intangible assets, third party acquisition and divestiture related costs, restructuring charges, and certain other special items as necessary. In addition, it is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and
incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets, and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Net</FONT> Income Attributable to onsemi and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted
Earnings Per Share </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;net</FONT> income attributable to onsemi and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share allows management to evaluate the operating results of onsemi&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally, the amortization and impairments of intangible assets, expensing of appraised inventory fair market
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;non-recurring</FONT></FONT> facility costs, restructuring, gains and losses on debt
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture related costs, tax indemnification by third
parties, tax impact of these items and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">other&nbsp;non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments, and certain other special items, as necessary. In addition, these items are important components of management&#146;s internal
performance measurement and incentive and reward process, as they are used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, setting targets, and forecasting future results.
Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures to enable investors and analysts to understand the results of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses and, to the extent comparable, to
compare our results of operations on a more consistent basis against those of other companies in our industry. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Free Cash Flow </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of free cash flow allows management to evaluate, among other things, the ability of the Company to make interest or principal payments
on its debt. Free cash flow is defined as the difference between cash flow from operating activities and capital expenditures disclosed under investing activities in the consolidated statement of cash flows. Free cash flow is not an alternate to
cash flow from operating </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NON-GAAP MEASURES (Continued) </B></P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
activities as a measure of liquidity. It is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and
historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets, and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT>
measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted Share Count </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count allows management to evaluate, among other things, the
potential dilution due to the outstanding stock options and restricted stock units excluding the dilution from the convertible notes that is covered by hedging activity up to a certain threshold. In periods when the quarterly average stock price per
share exceeds $20.72, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> share count&nbsp;includes the anti-dilutive impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 1.625% convertible notes. As such,
at an average stock price per share between $20.72 and $30.70, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 1.625% convertible notes. In periods when the quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $52.97, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> share count&nbsp;includes the anti-dilutive impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 0% convertible notes. As such, at an average stock price per
share between $52.97 and $74.34, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 0% convertible notes. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

</DIV></Center>
